| 1:07:56| Eventually, we get a piece of property that looked like this in the early to mid-1900s.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4076.4)|

| 1:08:10| It's pretty big because there are lots of ways people could get into| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4090.32)|
| 1:08:14| what was the state asylum in those days, and some of them weren't very nice.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4094.56)|
| 1:08:20| If a husband was mad at a wife, or someone wanted to steal nice farmland from a relative,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4100.32)|

| 1:15:17| Only two hours were on mobile crisis.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4517.04)|
| 1:15:19| So what it's literally telling new officers is, guess what?| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4519.28)|

| 1:15:27| And that's really over-skewing things.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4527.36)|
| 1:15:30| Because the illnesses are real, diagnosable, and treatable.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4530.24)|
| 1:15:33| And most people with mental illnesses live in the community.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4533.6)|
| 1:15:36| They're your family members, your friends, your colleagues,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4536.8)|
| 1:15:39| your neighbors, et cetera.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4539.04)|
| 1:15:40| So it was over-skewed.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4540.32)|

| 1:16:04| persons with lived experience, and colleagues| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4564.24)|
| 1:16:06| like our friends here at MCDAB Center| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4566.84)|
| 1:16:11| to provide the right type of training| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4571.2)|
| 1:16:13| so officers could understand mental illness better,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4573.36)|
| 1:16:16| so they could recognize it, so then they could| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4576.08)|
| 1:16:18| start the diversion process.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4578.48)|
| 1:16:21| That is a precursor for all sorts of good things| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-230803-joint-meeting?start=4581.5199999999995)|
